Residents are only allowed to park their cars inside their garage & one outside unless they pay for another garage or another outside permit sticker. Nobody follows the rules they're people that sublet, bring work vehicles home, or have multiple cars that all park outside without the permit all the time on top of the residents that don't work there's no parking in the afternoon & you'll have to park in far back lots or outside the gated community prone to crime with no eyes in sight. In the back lots people from swan lake jump over & break into cars & even steal gas out of them. The gate doesn't mean anything people that don't have a right to be in the community just wait in the nearby lot or even park right in front of the gate until a resident tries to come in & has to open it sometimes even has to get out of their vehicle so the sensor can detect it. There's no security, swan lake has better security than this place will ever have. There's other communities I'd suggest such as the Lewis property in Chino hills or the new townhomes in Ontario ranch road that have mortgages the same price as it is to rent here. I thought this place was amazing at first but as soon as I moved in you notice the problems & all the residents here say the same thing.

I'd look up the homecoming neighborhood watch page so you can see all the daily crime & issues that don't get resolved.

<user>114954925129440943399</user><Resp>None</Resp><text>WOW! Three words: crying. tiger. beef.
Try it and you won't regret it!

This place has a nicer ambiance than most kosher eateries on Pico, and the service is great. The place is tiny -- it probably fits  less than 40 people at most, so if you come with a group, have a reservation or be prepared to wait a while.

I came with a group of 5 girls and we had the chicken satay skewers with peanut sauce to start, 2 entrees of the crying tiger beef with sticky white rice, pad see ew (pictured), and the thai basil with chicken and rice (pictured). Pad see ew is one of my ultimate favorite thai dishes, or any cuisine for that matter, and this place just didn't do it for me. The noodles were short and thick, almost home-made looking, but not as satisfying. The crying beef was so tender and delicious; there's this citrusy spicy tangy clear sauce that goes on top mmmm mmm mmmmm. That made the dish in my opinion. The thai basil chicken was also very good.

I'll be back!<//text><Pictures>None<//Pictures><gmapID>0x80c2b954cf487c07:0xf3c3553b59937ade<//gmapID><Rating>5</Rating><name>Nicole Kohan</name></record></dataset><record>
